<li><cite class="citation book" id="CITEREFBurkett2002">Burkett, Delbert (2002). <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=EcsQknxV-xQC&amp;printsec=frontcover" rel="nofollow"><i>An Introduction to the New Testament and the Origins of Christianity</i></a>. Cambridge University Press. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-521-00720-7" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-521-00720-7">978-0-521-00720-7</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ANew+Testament&amp;rft.aufirst=Delbert&amp;rft.aulast=Burkett&amp;rft.btitle=An+Introduction+to+the+New+Testament+and+the+Origins+of+Christianity&amp;rft.date=2002&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-521-00720-7&amp;rft.pub=Cambridge+University+Press&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DEcsQknxV-xQC%26printsec%3Dfrontcover&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></li>
<li>von Campenhausen, Hans (1972). <i>The Formation of the Christian Bible</i>, English translation. Philadelphia: Fortress Press.</li>
<li>Clark, Gordon (1990). "Logical Criticisms of Textual Criticism", The Trinity Foundation: Jefferson, Maryland</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hans_Conzelmann" title="Hans Conzelmann">Conzelmann, Hans</a>; Lindemann, Andreas (1999). <i>Interpreting the New Testament: An Introduction to the Principles and Methods of New Testament Exegesis</i>, English translation. Peabody, Massachusetts: Hendrickson.</li>
<li>Dormeyer, Detlev (1998). <i>The New Testament among the Writings of Antiquity</i>, English translation. Sheffield.</li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Bart_D._Ehrman" title="Bart D. Ehrman">Ehrman, Bart D.</a> (2011). <i>The New Testament: A Historical Introduction to the Early Christian Writings</i>, 5th edition. New York: Oxford University Press.</li>
<li><cite class="citation book" id="CITEREFEhrman2005"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bart_D_Ehrman" title="Bart D Ehrman">Ehrman, Bart D.</a> (2005). <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=URdACxKubDIC&amp;printsec=frontcover" rel="nofollow"><i>Lost Christianities: The Battles for Scripture and the Faiths We Never Knew</i></a>. <li><a href="/wiki/Edgar_J._Goodspeed" title="Edgar J. Goodspeed">Goodspeed, Edgar J.</a> (1937). <i>An Introduction to the New Testament</i>. Chicago: University of Chicago Press.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amy-Jill_Levine" title="Amy-Jill Levine">Levine, Amy-Jill</a>; <a href="/wiki/Marc_Zvi_Brettler" title="Marc Zvi Brettler">Brettler, Marc Z.</a> (2011). <i>The Jewish Annotated New Testament</i>. Oxford: Oxford University Press.</li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="General_references">General references</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=New_Testament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: General references">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.ntgateway.com/" rel="nofollow">New Testament Gateway</a> Annotated guide to academic New Testament Web resources including not only other Web sites, but articles and course materials</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://JewishStudies.eteacherbiblical.com/" rel="nofollow">Jewish Studies for Christians</a> An Online Study Group exploring the Jewish setting of the early Jesus movement. (An Israeli blog led by Dr. Eliyahu Lizorkin-Eyzenberg).</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://oyc.yale.edu/religious-studies/introduction-to-new-testament" rel="nofollow">"Introduction to New Testament History and Literature" course materials</a> "Open Yale course" taught at Yale University by Dale B. Martin</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.tyndale.ca/seminary/mtsmodular/reading-rooms/newt" rel="nofollow">New Testament Reading Room</a>: Extensive on-line New Testament resources (including reference works, commentaries, translations, atlases, language tools, and works on New Testament theology), Tyndale Seminary</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.biblicalstudies.org.uk/nt.php" rel="nofollow">Biblicalstudies.org New Testament pages</a> Bibliographies on the New Testament and its individual books</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://bible.christianity.com/Lexicons/NewTestamentGreek/" rel="nofollow">Christianity.com Bible Study Tools</a> For-profit, conservative religious site with links to translations, as well as to mostly out-dated and non-critical commentaries, concordances, and other reference works</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.wlsessays.net/subject/N/New+Testament" rel="nofollow">Pastoral articles on the New Testament for ministerial training</a> Wisconsin Lutheran Seminary (WELS)</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.haaretz.com/culture/books/that-most-jewish-of-books-1.427292" rel="nofollow">Jewish reading of the New Testament</a> Haaretz essay on reclaiming the New Testament as an integral part of Jewish literature</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Development_and_authorship">Development and authorship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=New_Testament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Development and authorship">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.religioustolerance.org/chr_ntb1.htm" rel="nofollow">The Gospels</a> in the official canon, and some that were not included in the Bible</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.errantskeptics.org/DatingNT.htm" rel="nofollow">Dating the New Testament</a> A compilation of the dates ascribed by <a href="/wiki/Argumentum_ad_populum" title="Argumentum ad populum">various scholars</a> to the composition of the New Testament documents, accompanied by an odd statistical average of the dates</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Greek">Greek</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=New_Testament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Greek">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.ellopos.net/elpenor/greek-texts/new-testament/default.asp" rel="nofollow">New Testament Koine Greek Original</a> Side by side with the English (King James) and <a href="/wiki/Russian_Synodal_Bible" title="Russian Synodal Bible">Russian (Synodal) translation</a> Commentary by the Greek Fathers – Icons from <a href="/wiki/Mount_Athos" title="Mount Athos">Mount Athos</a></li>
